in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTexMouth_ST.xy + _MainTexMouth_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;

bool u_xlatb47;
float u_xlat48;
float u_xlat51;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat10_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat10_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat10_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1 = max(u_xlat1, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1 = inversesqrt(u_xlat1);

    u_xlatb47 = u_xlat47<u_xlat6.z;
    u_xlat6.x = (u_xlatb47) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat47 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlat47<u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat6.y = (u_xlatb47) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat47 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb47 = u_xlat47<u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat6.z = (u_xlatb47) ? 0.0 : 1.0;

    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;

    u_xlat21.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat15.zxy) + (-u_xlat21.xyz);

    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_44 * _Emissive;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;

    u_xlat16_45 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_45);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);

    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;

#else

#endif

    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_16 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_16 = min(max(u_xlat16_16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_16 = clamp(u_xlat16_16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat47 = u_xlat16_46 * u_xlat16_46;

    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);

    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);

        u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30;
        u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat5.x;
        u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
        u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati28).xyz;
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
        u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    }
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat11.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xx * u_xlat11.xy;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat16_2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTexMouth_ST.xy + _MainTexMouth_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;

vec4 u_xlat0;
bool u_xlatb0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_14.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_14.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb12 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb12 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb12 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14.x = min(max(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14.x = clamp(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat12.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_26.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));

    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));

    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_14.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb12 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb12 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb12 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14.x = min(max(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14.x = clamp(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat12.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_26.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_26.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_26.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_26.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_26.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_26.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_26.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat12.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_26.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_26.x = abs(u_xlat16_26.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat0.xx * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat4.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_5.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_26.y = max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_26.xy = min(u_xlat16_26.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_26.y) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_26.y * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat4.xy, u_xlat16_39).xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_26.y * u_xlat16_26.y;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_26.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_26.x = (-u_xlat16_26.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_19.x = u_xlat16_5.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_19.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_19.x = u_xlat16_19.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_19.x = min(max(u_xlat16_19.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_19.x = clamp(u_xlat16_19.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_26.y) + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_31 = min(max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_19.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = (-u_xlat16_6.xyz) * u_xlat16_19.xxx + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat37 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat37;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat37);
    u_xlat5.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat40 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = max(u_xlat5.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_19.xyz = u_xlat16_7.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_19.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _SHColorScale.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_5.z));
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_5.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_43 = u_xlat16_43 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_43 = exp2(u_xlat16_43);
    u_xlat16_43 = min(u_xlat16_43, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_43) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_26.y * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat16_26.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat13 * u_xlat13;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat1.xzw * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xxx + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14.x = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_14.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xxx * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_9.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14.x = min(max(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_43 = min(u_xlat16_43, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_43) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_26.y * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat16_26.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat13 * u_xlat13;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat1.xzw * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xxx + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14.x = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_14.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xxx * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14.x = clamp(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xxx * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = max(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = min(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_14.x = (-u_xlat13) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_26.x * u_xlat16_14.x + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_26.x / u_xlat16_14.x;
    u_xlat16_26.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_26.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_26.x);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_26.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_26.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_26.x = clamp(u_xlat16_26.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_26.x = u_xlat16_43 * u_xlat16_26.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_14.x * u_xlat16_26.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_26.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_26.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_26.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_26.x * u_xlat16_14.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = clamp(u_xlat16_14.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_26.x = u_xlat16_14.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_14.x * u_xlat16_14.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_14.x * u_xlat16_26.x;
    u_xlat16_26.x = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_26.x + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_14.x;
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = u_xlat10_6.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat10_6.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat10_6.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_12.xyz * u_xlat10_6.www;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;

vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTexMouth_ST.xy + _MainTexMouth_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTexMouth_ST.xy + _MainTexMouth_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
vec3 u_xlat13;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
float u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
float u_xlat38;
float u_xlat39;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat13.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat13.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat13.zxy) * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat13.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = abs(u_xlat16_36) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat4.xy * u_xlat16_6.xx;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat16_6.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_18.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_18.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = textureLod(_MatMap, u_xlat3.xy, u_xlat16_18.x).xyz;
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_18.x * u_xlat16_18.x;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_42 = (-u_xlat16_30) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_30 = min(max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_42 = (-u_xlat16_42) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_42 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_42 = min(max(u_xlat16_42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_42 = clamp(u_xlat16_42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_19.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_30) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat38;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat38);
    u_xlat4.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat39 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_18.xy = max(u_xlat4.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_18.xy = u_xlat16_18.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_18.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xyz * _SHColorScale.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_4.z));
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_22 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_10.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_10.x = exp2(u_xlat16_10.x);
    u_xlat16_10.x = min(u_xlat16_10.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xyz * u_xlat16_19.xyz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18.x = _SHshadow + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_18.x = min(max(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_18.x = clamp(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat2.x;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);

    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif

#endif

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OcclusionStrength;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_TARGET0;

{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
